check this post  
  
[http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...72#post4790872](http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?p=4790872#post4790872)  
  
  
I have posted an EA that takes signals from supertrend/ trend magic. If we could incorporate a filter of macbb in that EA, this system would be worthwhile.  
  
Long and short signals as per supertrend signal and macdbb to filter countertrend trades.  
  
Strategy is to open 2 or multiple of 2 lots....take partial profits at 10 pips or so and allow other lots to run till the supertrend signal lasts.  
  
We can just put the EA and switch it on /off as per macdbb.  
  
Anybody interested in modifying this EA as per this system?

> [Quoting Jani72](/thread/post/4684105#post4684105 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> I'm not sure how the current TM works, but atleast the one i used a while ago had a redrawing issue.  
>    
>  Problem with TM comes when CCI crosses 0-level and TM will redraw, so what you see on history chart is not what you see on live trading!   
>    
>  I used TM (actually just CCI) in one EA and solved the redrawing by programming a parameter for treshold margin around 0-level, so inside this margin no buy/sell signals are given only on crossing treshold up or down and if treshold set to 0 indi works as original. For example if treshold set to 20 indi...
> 
> Ignored

Hi, Jani72. That's very interesting. Can you share your customised CCI indicator?  
  
Thank you, in anticipation.

Austin is pretty close to Karl Dittmann and this fact alone should make everyone careful about "his" products...  
Well, the news is that now he is selling this Indestructible Trend Winner that is a lousy copy of this Trend Magic or Forex Simplification System that is also available here <http://www.forexbees.com/forex-simplification-system/> for free.  
The only difference is that he added the fractals to set Stop Losses and a yellow line between the red (sell) and the green (buy) lines to warn you that a change of colour is probably about to happen.  
Look at the two charts: one is made with Austin's indicator and the other one is made with Trend Magic template. Pretty the same, eh?  
The settings are the same as well: CCI 50 and ATR 5.  
  
So my advice is: save your bucks and keep on with this system that is much better than Austin's one ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1)

  * | Joined Aug 2013  | Status: Trader | [172 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=346943)

Ended up taking 21.2pips on CHF/JPY trade and 15 pips on EUR/JPY trade because i wanted to go to bed and i am yet to get over leaving trades in while i go to bed when no profit is locked in... CHF/JPY the lowest low was 31pips and using the system you would have gotten 14pips as for EUR/JPY lowest low was 37pips from when i enterd the trade and following the system would have been 15pips...  
  
I also believe its all in how you use your stoploss in any system and how your emotions are trading the plan, with the aud/nzd i pulled out early because i felt the price was oscillating, as soon as i closed it the price fell my way to 60pips on 15min time frame if i didn't interfere with that particular trade.  
  
i have placed 6 trades using this system so far...  
EUR/JPY 20.9 pips profit  
CHF/JPY 4.8 pips profit  
EUR/CAD 14 pips loss  
AUD/NZD 5.2pips profit  
CHF/JPY 21.2 pips profit  
EUR/JPY 15 pips profit  
  
i entered on the candle after the yellow vertical line

  * [ fxforecast](fxforecast)

  * | Commercial User  | Joined Jan 2016 | [99 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=440892)

Hi everyone, I am a technical analyst using technical trend lines to predict price movements. I can develop a chart template for any currency for use on mt4 platform.  
  
_For EURUSD 4th-8th January 2016_  
  
_

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: EURUSDH4trend.png
Size: 42 KB](/attachment/image/1823269/thumbnail?d=1451985818)](/attachment/image/1823269?d=1451985818)   

_  
The trend is clearly bearish as outlined by the white trendline; the redlines outline the support trendline, price may reverse on the redlines, a break through them will open further fall in price. The green trendlines are current resistance line and the yellow lines simulate a possible price movement.  
  
EURUSDTrendForecast template is attached. You can save it in the template folder to attach it on mt4 chart.  
  
The chart can be viewed on 4hrs, 1hrs, and 30min time-frames.  

Attached File(s)

![File Type: tpl](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/tpl.gif) [EURUSDTrendForecast.tpl](/attachment/file/1823274?d=1451986072) 4 KB | 277 downloads

Put the file inside the template folder located inside the Mt4 installation folder. The name of the folder to put the file is Template, after then you go to the mt4 trading terminal, and click on the template menu to select the template from the list.

Attached Image

![](/attachment/image/1828376?d=1452543648)

_EUR/USD 11th - 15th January 2016 Review._  
Following the expectation of the price simulating yellow line, a sell order was opened at 1.0911, with take profit at 1.0840.  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: EURUSDH4TRADE.png
Size: 51 KB](/attachment/image/1828964/thumbnail?d=1452610331)](/attachment/image/1828964?d=1452610331)   

  
  
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 4hoursEURUSD1-12-2016.png
Size: 46 KB](/attachment/image/1828968/thumbnail?d=1452610538)](/attachment/image/1828968?d=1452610538)   

  
The profit target 1.0840 was taken as expected. Now the price movement calls for caution because the bear force still exists between the red dotted trend lines. If the price can maintain a close above the support of 1.0800 between January 12, 2016 and the open of trading for the European session on January 14, 2016, the bull should break out of the red dotted line. The blue simulating line shows bear force exist within the price range of 1.0900 and 1.0800.

I develop an expert advisor to forecast EURUSD & GBPUSD technical analysis. Download the EA and attach it to 4hour timeframe on EURUSD and 1hour time frame on GBPUSD.  
  
Due to metatrader different build or version you have to download the specific EA for your mt4 version.

Attached File(s)

![File Type: ex4](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/ex4.gif) [TrendForecast.ex4](/attachment/file/1839424?d=1453807266) 27 KB | 352 downloads

Attached File(s)

![File Type: zip](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/zip.gif) [TrendForecastBuild765.zip](/attachment/file/1839425?d=1453807313) 25 KB | 207 downloads

Attached File(s)

![File Type: zip](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/zip.gif) [TrendForecastBuild950.zip](/attachment/file/1839495?d=1453811994) 26 KB | 243 downloads 

  
When loading the EA, ignore the Email and Password input and click OK to load TrendForecast.ex4, DLL import most be allowed on the mt4 terminal for the EA to work.

Ok, I noticed the mt4 terminal you are using identified the EURUSD pairs and GBPUSD pairs as "EURUSDi" and "GBPUSDi" respectively, the TrendForecast.ex4 will only recongnise "EURUSD" without the "i". That is why it won't load. The solution now is to load another EURUSD chart and GBPUSD chart without "i".

If the EA keeps printing DLL not allowed, then the DLL is not enabled on the terminal. I am using the EA on thesame Tradersway mt4 terminal and it works.   
I think the DLL is not enabled on the mt4 terminal, it may be enabled on the EA settings but may not be enabled on the mt4 terminal.  

Attached Image

![](/attachment/image/1841723?d=1453994702)

  
Go to Tools in the mt4 menu and select options, then now navigate to the Expert Advisor menu to check if the DLL is enabled and retry to load the EA again. I attached some screen shot below.

  * Edited 6:31pm  Feb 8, 2016 5:33pm | Edited 6:31pm 

  * [ fxforecast](fxforecast)

  * | Commercial User  | Joined Jan 2016 | [99 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=440892)

A new feature has been added to the Trend Forecast technical analysis, called the "Trade-Time-Zones". The Trade-Time-Zones shows the Trend entry and exit point in time period. Price can make an entry point for a trend or take profit for an exit at the Trade-Time-Zones. When price start to make a correction around the Trade-Time-Zones, it's a good opportunity to exit or enter a trade.  
  
MT4 Build 765 

Attached File(s)

![File Type: zip](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/zip.gif) [TrendForecastBuild765.zip](/attachment/file/1850484?d=1454920280) 25 KB | 223 downloads 

  
  
MT4 Build 910 

Attached File(s)

![File Type: zip](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/zip.gif) [TrendForecastBuild910.zip](/attachment/file/1850485?d=1454920295) 26 KB | 233 downloads 

  
  
MT4 Build 950 

Attached File(s)

![File Type: zip](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/zip.gif) [TrendForecastBuild950.zip](/attachment/file/1850486?d=1454920306) 27 KB | 330 downloads 

  
  
When attaching the EA to chart, ignore the INPUTS required and click OK button to load it and Allow DLL function must be enabled for the EA to work.

A new version of Trend Forecast EA is available, the TrendForecast_v1.2.ex4. The Trial version is attached below; it works on both 1hour and 4hour timeframe on EURUSD, GBPUSD, AUDUSD and NZDUSD. In the new version, when a trader switch between 1hour and 4hour time frames the EA will re-display the trend lines to suit each timeframe.  
  
_**EURUSD 4HOUR TIME FRAME**_  
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: EURUSDH4v1.2.png
Size: 42 KB](/attachment/image/1876820/thumbnail?d=1457611694)](/attachment/image/1876820?d=1457611694)   

  
  
  
_**EURUSD 1HOUR TIME FRAME**_  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

**_A little detail about the triangle trend line_**   
  
The triangle trend line identifies the current market bull and bear force. When the triangle is facing up the price is actively bullish then when the price cross into the triangle facing down the bear force is active. This help to identify when to buy and sell a trade.  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: GBPUSDH43-29-2016.png
Size: 50 KB](/attachment/image/1890694/thumbnail?d=1459233182)](/attachment/image/1890694?d=1459233182)   

  
Any questions and comment regarding the trend forecast is welcomed.

_**GBPUSD Forecast for 30th March 2016**_.  
  
_LONG PATTERN_  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: LONG PATTERN.PNG
Size: 52 KB](/attachment/image/1892082/thumbnail?d=1459332810)](/attachment/image/1892082?d=1459332810)   

  
  
The current bullish triangle facing up is currently overbought for the 1.4501 level; it will be more comfortable for the price to correct into the next bullish triangle facing up; indicated in the LONG PATTERN image, to trade for the 1.4501 level on route for 1.4569 level. Any price push up towards the 1.4501 level in the current bullish triangle will be a risk on trade.  
  
_SHORT PATTERN_  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: SHORT PATTERN.PNG
Size: 51 KB](/attachment/image/1892084/thumbnail?d=1459332826)](/attachment/image/1892084?d=1459332826)   

  
  
And for a sell trade to occur, the price has to break through the now support green trend line as indicated in the SHORT PATTERN image to target the 1.4283 level.

_**EURUSD**_

**_GBPUSD Forecast Update 31st March- 1st April 2016._**  
  
A interesting formation pop up from my trading archive on EURUSD within the period 2015.05.11 to 2015.06.30, something similar may occur tomorrow on GBPUSD, so trading tomorrow especially at the non-farm payroll release calls for caution.
